Particles of dust swarm the room, blocking your sight. The soft sound of 
leathery wings rustling in the darkness echoes through the cave, denoting the 
presence of bats. During the day, a thin shaft of light penetrates a few feet in
from the cave mouth to the south. From further south comes the low, soft babble 
of running water. Like sharp teeth, a few stalagmites reach up from the ground 
here. A putrid golem of flesh and dirt towers over its surroundings here.

gruesome crescent scythe in his hands.
